const products = {
    1: { name: "ุนุจุงูุฉ ุณูุฏุงุก ูุทุฑุฒุฉ", price: 499 },
    2: { name: "ุนุจุงูุฉ ูุญูู ูุฒููุฉ", price: 599 }
};

// ุนุฑุถ ูุญุชููุงุช ุงูุณูุฉ
function renderCart() {
    const cartItems = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
    const cartContainer = document.getElementById('cart-items');
    let total = 0;

    cartContainer.innerHTML = cartItems.map(item => `
        <div class="cart-item">
            <h3>${products[item.id].name}</h3>
            <p>ุงูุณุนุฑ: ${products[item.id].price} ุฌููู</p>
            <div class="quantity-controls">
                <button onclick="updateQuantity(${item.id}, -1)">-</button>
                <span>${item.quantity}</span>
                <button onclick="updateQuantity(${item.id}, 1)">+</button>
            </div>
            <button onclick="removeItem(${item.id})">ุญุฐู</button>
        </div>
    `).join('');

    // ุญุณุงุจ ุงูุฅุฌูุงูู
    total = cartItems.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (products[item.id].price * item.quantity), 0);
    document.getElementById('total').textContent = total;
}

// ุชุญุฏูุซ ุงููููุฉ
function updateQuantity(productId, change) {
    let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
    const item = cart.find(item => item.id === productId);
    
    if (item) {
        item.quantity += change;
        if (item.quantity <= 0) cart = cart.filter(i => i.id !== productId);
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        renderCart();
    }
}

// ุญุฐู ููุชุฌ
function removeItem(productId) {
    let cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
    cart = cart.filter(item => item.id !== productId);
    localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
    renderCart();
}

// ุงูุชุญููู ุงูุฃููู
window.onload = renderCart;

// ุนุฏูุงุฏ ุชูุงุฒูู ููุนุฑุถ
function updateCounter() {
    const endDate = new Date("2024-12-31");
    const now = new Date();
    const diff = endDate - now;
    
    const days = Math.floor(diff / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    document.getElementById("days").textContent = days;
}

// ุฅุถุงูุฉ ููุณูุฉ ูุน ุฎุงุตูุฉ ุงููููููุดู

    button.addEventListener("click", function() {
        const productId = this.getAttribute("data-id");
        const cart = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("cart")) || [];
        
        cart.push({
            id: productId,
            collection: "new-2024",
            quantity: 1
        });
        
        localStorage.setItem("cart", JSON.stringify(cart));
        alert("ุชูุช ุงูุฅุถุงูุฉ ุฅูู ุณูุฉ ุงูุชุณูู!");
    });
});

ูู new-collection.js:
javascript
Copy
// ูุธุงู ุงูุฅุนุฌุงุจุงุช
document.querySelectorAll('.like-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const productId = this.getAttribute('data-product-id');
        let likes = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('likes')) || {};
        
        if (!likes[productId]) {
            likes[productId] = 1;
            this.classList.add('liked');
        } else {
            delete likes[productId];
            this.classList.remove('liked');
        }
        
        localStorage.setItem('likes', JSON.stringify(likes));
        this.querySelector('.like-count').textContent = likes[productId] || 0;
    });
});

// ุชุญููู ุงูุฅุนุฌุงุจุงุช ุนูุฏ ุงูุจุฏุก
window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    const likes = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('likes')) || {};
    document.querySelectorAll('.like-btn').forEach(btn => {
        const productId = btn.getAttribute('data-product-id');
        if (likes[productId]) {
            btn.classList.add('liked');
            btn.querySelector('.like-count').textContent = likes[productId];
        }
    });
});

// ุชุฃุซูุฑุงุช ุญุฑููุฉ ุนูุฏ ุงูุชูุฑูุฑ
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // ุชุฃุซูุฑ ุธููุฑ ุงูุนูุงุตุฑ ุนูุฏ ุงูุชูุฑูุฑ
    const animateOnScroll = function() {
        const elements = document.querySelectorAll('.team-member, .stat-card');
        
        elements.forEach(element => {
            const elementPosition = element.getBoundingClientRect().top;
            const screenPosition = window.innerHeight / 1.3;
            
            if (elementPosition < screenPosition) {
                element.style.opacity = '1';
                element.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
            }
        });
    };
    
    // ุฅุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุนูุงุตุฑ ูุจู ุงูุธููุฑ
    const setupAnimation = function() {
        const elements = document.querySelectorAll('.team-member, .stat-card');
        
        elements.forEach(element => {
            element.style.opacity = '0';
            element.style.transform = 'translateY(20px)';
            element.style.transition = 'all 0.6s ease';
        });
    };
    
    setupAnimation();
    window.addEventListener('scroll', animateOnScroll);
    animateOnScroll(); // ุชุดุบูู ูุฑุฉ ุฃููู ุนูุฏ ุงูุชุญููู
});

// ุชูุนูู ุฃุฒุฑุงุฑ ุงููุดุงุฑูุฉ

    const animateOnScroll = function() {
        const elements = document.querySelectorAll('.contact-form, .contact-info, .map-section');
        
        elements.forEach(element => {
            const elementPosition = element.getBoundingClientRect().top;
            const screenPosition = window.innerHeight / 1.3;
            
            if (elementPosition < screenPosition) {
                element.style.opacity = '1';
                element.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
            }
        });
    };
    
    // ุฅุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุนูุงุตุฑ ูุจู ุงูุธููุฑ
    const setupAnimation = function() {

        elements.forEach(element => {

            element.style.transform = 'translateY(20px)';
            element.style.transition = 'all 0.6s ease';
        });
    };

    const menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('.menu-item');
    
    menuItems.forEach(item => {
        const title = item.querySelector('.menu-title');
        
        title.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            item.classList.toggle('active');
            
            // ุฅุบูุงู ุจุงูู ุงูููุงุฆู ุงููุฑุนูุฉ

                menuItems.forEach(otherItem => {
                    if (otherItem !== item && otherItem.classList.contains('active')) {
                        otherItem.classList.remove('active');
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
    
    // ุชูุนูู ููุชุฑ ุงูุฃููุงู

    const animateOnScroll = function() {
        const elements = document.querySelectorAll('.product-card');
        
        elements.forEach(element => {
            const elementPosition = element.getBoundingClientRect().top;
            const screenPosition = window.innerHeight / 1.3;
            
            if (elementPosition < screenPosition) {
                element.style.opacity = '1';
                element.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
            }
        });
    };
    
    // ุฅุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุนูุงุตุฑ ูุจู ุงูุธููุฑ
    const setupAnimation = function() {
        const elements = document.querySelectorAll('.product-card');
        
        elements.forEach(element => {
            element.style.opacity = '0';
            element.style.transform = 'translateY(20px)';
            element.style.transition = 'all 0.6s ease';
        });
    };
    
    setupAnimation();
    window.addEventListener('scroll', animateOnScroll);
    animateOnScroll(); // ุชุดุบูู ูุฑุฉ ุฃููู ุนูุฏ ุงูุชุญููู

    const animateOnScroll = function() {
        const elements = document.querySelectorAll('.product-card, .feature-card');
        
        elements.forEach((element, index) => {
            const elementPosition = element.getBoundingClientRect().top;
            const screenPosition = window.innerHeight / 1.3;
            
            if (elementPosition < screenPosition) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    element.style.opacity = '1';
                    element.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
                }, index * 100);
            }
        });
    };
    
    // ุฅุนุฏุงุฏ ุงูุนูุงุตุฑ ูุจู ุงูุธููุฑ
    const setupAnimation = function() {
        const elements = document.querySelectorAll('.product-card, .feature-card');
        
        elements.forEach(element => {
            element.style.opacity = '0';
            element.style.transform = 'translateY(20px)';
            element.style.transition = 'all 0.6s ease';
        });
    };
    
    setupAnimation();
    window.addEventListener('scroll', animateOnScroll);
    animateOnScroll(); // ุชุดุบูู ูุฑุฉ ุฃููู ุนูุฏ ุงูุชุญููู

            if (this.classList.contains('active')) {
                this.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-heart"></i>';

    function renderOrderDetails(orderNumber, data) {
        let statusSteps = '';
        let productsList = '';
        
        // ุชุญุฏูุฏ ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุทูุจ

            preparing: { icon: 'fa-tshirt', text: 'ููุฏ ุงูุชุฌููุฒ', active: true },
            shipping: { icon: 'fa-truck', text: 'ุงูุดุญู', active: false },
            delivered: { icon: 'fa-home', text: 'ุงูุชุณููู', active: false }

        for (const [key, step] of Object.entries(statusConfig)) {
            const isCompleted = key === 'received' || (key === 'preparing' && data.status !== 'received');
            const isActive = key === data.status;
            
            statusSteps += `

                    </div>

        data.products.forEach(product => {

                    <img src="${product.image}" alt="${product.name}">

                        <h3>${product.name}</h3>
                        <p>ุงููููุฉ: ${product.quantity}</p>

            `;
        });
        
        // ุนุฑุถ ูู ุงูุจูุงูุงุช
        document.getElementById('order-status').innerHTML = `

                <div class="order-summary">
                    <h3>ููุฎุต ุงูุทูุจ</h3>
                    <div class="summary-row">
                        <span>ุงูุฅุฌูุงูู</span>
                        <span>${data.products.reduce((sum, p) => sum + (p.price * p.quantity), 0)} ุฌ.ู</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="summary-row">
                        <span>ุงูุดุญู</span>
                        <span>${data.shipping} ุฌ.ู</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="summary-row total">
                        <span>ุงููุจูุบ ุงูููุงุฆู</span>
                        <span>${data.products.reduce((sum, p) => sum + (p.price * p.quantity), 0) + data.shipping} ุฌ.ู</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }
    
    // (ุงุฎุชูุงุฑู) ุฌูุจ ุฑูู ุงูุทูุจ ูู URL ุฅุฐุง ูุงู ููุฌูุฏุงู

        document.getElementById('track-btn').click();
    }

        const orderRef = firebase.database().ref('orders/' + orderNumber);
        
        orderRef.once('value')
            .then((snapshot) => {
                const orderData = snapshot.val();
                
                if (!orderData) {
                    orderStatusDiv.innerHTML = `
                        <div class="error">
                            <i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle"></i>
                            <p>ูุง ููุฌุฏ ุทูุจ ุจูุฐุง ุงูุฑูู!</p>
                        </div>
                    `;
                    return;
                }

                // ุนุฑุถ ุจูุงูุงุช ุงูุทูุจ
                renderOrder(orderNumber, orderData);
            })
            .catch((error) => {
                orderStatusDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="error">
                        <i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle"></i>
                        <p>ุญุฏุซ ุฎุทุฃ: ${error.message}</p>
                    </div>
                `;
            });
    });

    function renderOrder(orderNumber, order) {
        // ุชุญููู ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุทูุจ ุฅูู ุฎุทูุงุช
        const statusSteps = {
            'ุฌุฏูุฏ': { icon: 'fa-shopping-cart', done: true },
            'ููุฏ ุงูุชุฌููุฒ': { icon: 'fa-box-open', done: order.status !== 'ุฌุฏูุฏ' },
            'ุชู ุงูุดุญู': { icon: 'fa-truck', done: order.status === 'ุชู ุงูุดุญู' },
            'ุชู ุงูุชุณููู': { icon: 'fa-check-circle', done: order.status === 'ุชู ุงูุชุณููู' }
        };

        let stepsHTML = '';
        for (const [status, info] of Object.entries(statusSteps)) {
            stepsHTML += `
                <div class="step ${info.done ? 'completed' : ''} ${order.status === status ? 'active' : ''}">
                    <div class="step-icon"><i class="fas ${info.icon}"></i></div>
                    <div class="step-text">
                        <h3>${status}</h3>
                        ${order.status === status ? `<p>${new Date().toLocaleDateString('ar-EG')}</p>` : ''}
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }

        // ุนุฑุถ ูู ุดูุก
        orderStatusDiv.innerHTML = `
            <div class="status-progress">
                ${stepsHTML}
            </div>
            <div class="order-details">
                <h2>ุชูุงุตูู ุงูุทูุจ #${orderNumber}</h2>
                <div class="product-info">
                    <p><strong>ุงูุนููู:</strong> ${order.customer || 'ุบูุฑ ูุนุฑูู'}</p>
                    <p><strong>ุงูุฅุฌูุงูู:</strong> ${order.total || order.price} ุฌ.ู</p>
                    <p><strong>ุชุงุฑูุฎ ุงูุทูุจ:</strong> ${order.date || new Date().toLocaleDateString('ar-EG')}</p>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }
});
